< userid>
112197715738916932243<//userid>
<gmap_id>0x80d957ffcdee700d:0x86fc0d037473216e</gmap_id><pics>None</pics>< Name>
Matthew Jakubczak<//Name>
< date>
1546321852260</date>
< Rating>
5<//Rating>
<Resp>None<//Resp>< text>
This place has become my family's favorite go-to for a good Christmas dinner. While I typically deplore the idea of making anyone work on such a holiday, I am not going to turn down a family dinner, and this place has earned our business 3 years running. The food is always very, very fresh. The ingredients are all very well picked, fresh, and you can taste the quality as opposed to many others. When going for Chinese lately it seems that Panda Express is about the level of quality you can expect in most places, where you can tell the meat is drowned in sauce to try and cover up the fact it is low quality, but not here. As far as I can tell, all the ingredients are what would be a first round choice, and they don't simply try to hide the flaws the meat or veggies may have by covering them with excessive sauce or a crunchy outer shell.

The actual restaurant has downsized a little from the first time we went, which unfortunately without a reservation could mean you will be stuck waiting for another party to finish before you can be seated. But the actual food os worth the wait, and while they don't blatantly rush you through your meal, they will make sure you're satisfied in a timely manner so they may serve other customers. We did not feel rushed, our drinks were kept full, and the food came relatively quickly, which made it easier to eat then go tour the Christmas lights around town. Even with the downsizing, the dining area was not cramped; in fact it seemed like the tables were spread out a little better adding to the comfort for the meal.

The menu is very comprehensive, guaranteed to have something for everyone, with pictures and actual brief descriptions so you arent left totally guessing what is what. I chose the Crispy Beef, which is similar albeit much better than Panda Express' Beijing Beef. The difference that stood out to me was the fact there were good chunks of beef, and what I assume was a rice wine vinegar in the sauce that gave it an almost pickled taste that really worked well.

If you are looking for a quality Chinese place around town, you surely cannot go wrong giving Panda Country a try.< /text>

<user_name>Matthew Contri<//user_name><Resp>None<//Resp>< UserId.>
108252553398502836661< /UserId.>
< review>
Today was the last straw for me with this place. I have been to this place on various occasions throughout the past two years for small items that I needed when in a bind and my supplier couldn't get it to me in time. And every time walked out empty handed and irritated. The sad part is I live 3 minutes away from this place and would rather drive to Rancho Cucamonga and shop at the candy supply store there then waste 1 penny on this place.

3 Reasons they received a 1 Star rating:

1) The store is small and very cluttered. The organization of the store will leave you wandering aroud trying to find everything.

2) All of the reviews about rudeness is true. The arrogance and inconvenience felt is very evident from everyone who works there.

3) This is the one that irritates me the most. The information given to customers in regards to Chocolate. I am not sure about their cake information they give out but as a professional chocolatier, I take great offense by the information they give their customers about chocolate. Merkins chocolate is in no way shape or form better than real chocolate. In a day when eating healthier is better and on the forefront of many peoples minds, Merkins chocolate which has 10+ ingredients (none of which are closely related to chocolate, in fact cocoa in most cases is not even an ingredient) is not better than the real chocolate which has at most 5 ingredients most of which is chocolate derivatives (i.e. cocoa powder, cocoa liquer, etc.) and the taste is WAY much better then the Merkins stuff. Also, with real chocolate and the Merkins "chocolate" you can add real ingredients into it for flavoring  (i.e. liquor, real fruits and such) unlike what the class tells you where "nothing can be added to chocolate except for oils because it will seize up" Wrong Wrong Wrong!!!

When a customer asks "How long will it take for the chocolate to set after dipping?" Don't answer, "Depending on room temperature, it should take no more than 5 minutes" Any type of chocolate, Merkins or the real deal cannot set properly at temps higher than 73 degrees, especially here in California. We don't have to worry about humidity as much but chocolate will take forever if at all to set at higher temperatures. Room Temperature is not a correct answer, in fact it is a very generalized answer that can and will ruin the chocolate confections you make if taken in the wrong context.

If you are here for cakes have fun, if you are here for chocolate turn around and run.</review>

<Rate>5</Rate>< Review>
The itself theater is great and the food is good, especially for a movie theater/restaurant combination. I had a hamburger at my last visit that was served quickly and met my expectations, and I've never had a problem with service or with the food I've eaten there.

I've often seen opening day movies and it's great fun to have food, a drink, and a movie at the same time. It's a great spot for a date or time with a good friend. It's pretty intimate, especially if you're eating while watching the movie, so it might not be perfect for a large group. That's probably part of why I like it so much.</Review>

Ran by a group of all differently interesting  personalites so insync with eachother that they effortlessly seem to manage and maintain ship to provide you the smooth stress free  experience you expect to have on an special outing event like going out to the Movie theater used to and should still be. I informed her I was a diabetic and could not eat the candy from the display. I asked for their corporate office, contact person and her name. Only then did she offer me two free movie passes. I told her I was satisfied with the free passes and didn't need to contact their corporate office but took the information anyway. I tried to use the tickets when Thor: Ragnarok came out and was informed by Carl that I could only use the ticket approximately 3-4 weeks after the movie came out. It was very frustrating to say the least. I still have the movie tickets and now I can't use them to see the Black Panther movie. This is some of the most horrible customer service I have experienced in a long time.< /review>
